- **A (Standard):** Developed {count} Ethereum smart contracts managing {tvl}+ TVL, cutting gas costs {gas}% per transaction and passing {audits} third-party audits with zero critical findings.
- **B (Result-first):** Cut gas costs {gas}% per transaction and passed {audits} audits with zero critical findings by developing {count} Ethereum smart contracts managing {tvl}+ TVL.
- **C (Impact-led):** Delivered {gas}% gas reduction and zero critical audit findings across {audits} audits; developed {count} Ethereum smart contracts securing {tvl}+ TVL.
- **D (Concise):** Built {count} Ethereum contracts managing {tvl}+ TVL, gas down {gas}%, {audits} audits passed with zero critical findings.
